| 0:02:00| Now a word about how discussion will take place.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=120)|
| 0:02:03| After each item is called, I'll read the staff's recommendation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=123)|
| 0:02:07| On certain items, I'll call on staff to comment.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=127)|
| 0:02:11| At this time, the applicant may address the commission or defer his or her opening remarks and allow any opposition to speak first.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=131)|
| 0:02:20| The applicant and those in support of the applicant will be given a total of five minutes to speak.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=140)|
| 0:02:26| I will then ask for other comments from the floor.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=146)|
| 0:02:29| The opposition will also be given a total of five minutes to speak.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=149)|
| 0:02:34| If either side wishes to have an opportunity for rebuttal, you'll need to reserve time from your allotted five minutes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=154)|
| 0:02:43| Applicants and citizens who registered to participate and are attending the meeting in person will be asked to come to the podium and share their name and address for the record where their item is heard.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=163)|
| 0:02:55| Those who have registered to speak online do not need to sign in at the podium.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=175)|
| 0:03:01| If you'd like to speak on an agenda item and have not registered to do so in advance, please raise your hand when the item is read to the record.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=181)|
| 0:03:10| I'll then indicate when it is time for you to speak and you can approach the podium at that time.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=190)|
| 0:03:16| You'll be asked to sign in at the podium as well as state your name and address for the record.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=196)|
| 0:03:21| If the Planning Commission decision on that item is appealed and we need to notify you, we cannot do so without your name and address.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=201)|
| 0:03:32| The Planning Commission may grant additional time for presentation of information.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=212)|
| 0:03:37| Speakers should limit their remarks to the facts of the case and should avoid repeating comments that have been previously presented to the Planning Commission.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=217)|
| 0:03:47| Because of the number of items that we have before us, groups in favor or opposed to an item have been asked to appoint a spokesperson to represent them.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=227)|

| 1:06:25| Our goal is to begin the process of creating more diverse housing options at a variety of price points for Knoxville residents.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=3985)|
| 1:06:34| As Mayor Kincannon indicated at the opening of the city council workshop last week, this is one piece, a small piece, of an overall housing strategy.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=3994)|
| 1:06:45| The intent is to bring forward a more comprehensive housing plan in a few months.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4005)|
| 1:06:50| Based on their experience with cities across the country, Optico's design emphasized that missing middle housing is not necessarily a good fit across all areas of town.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4010)|
| 1:07:01| And that cities with the most success have started with a limited geographic area that already has access to infrastructure like transit, it's walkable and bikeable, and has access to neighborhood servicing businesses.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4021)|
| 1:07:15| Traditional neighborhood residential, TDR, is described as a mix of detached and attached houses, often on smaller lots.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4035)|
| 1:07:25| TDR is walkable and bikeable, it aligns well with the CAT reimagined routes that will take effect next year, and residents have access to businesses close by.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4045)|
| 1:07:36| This is the geographic area that the plan is based on.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4056)|
| 1:07:40| I met with more than 40 individuals during the time we were working on the plan to gain insights before it launched the end of August.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4060)|
| 1:07:49| These included residents in the neighborhoods impacted, it included several local small residential contractors, as that is who is most likely to be building middle housing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4069)|
| 1:07:59| It also included many who are concerned about the need for housing in our community.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4079)|
| 1:08:04| While middle housing was not really designed specifically to be an affordable housing strategy, it does not mean it cannot be affordable.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4084)|
| 1:08:14| I have met with several of our local non-profit developers about this plan, and they're particularly excited to see this come to fruition.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4094)|
| 1:08:22| Since our plan launched via the city's website, in addition to the planning site, we've spoken with neighborhood groups, hosted two community open house events, and conducted a city council workshop.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4102)|
| 1:08:34| We appreciate the attendance of the community, and to those of you who were able to attend, we appreciate that as well.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4114)|

| 1:13:03| less maintenance per person, less cost, more connectivity, and more tax dollars per acre.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4383)|
| 1:13:10| Let's allow these benefits in all zones, and let's allow all people the freedom to determine where they live.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4390)|
| 1:13:21| Finally, demolitions and conversions should not be grounds to hold this proposal up.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4401)|
| 1:13:26| The cost of land acquisition and the actual cost of demolishing an existing home would rule out this scenario,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4406)|
| 1:13:34| unless that existing home is truly rotting and didn't hold much market value anyway.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4414)|
| 1:13:40| Conversions are extremely unlikely.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4420)|
| 1:13:45| Yet, the public is wary of this, and it makes sense.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4425)|
| 1:13:49| We've all seen historic homes get chopped up into thoughtless and unsafe apartments.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4429)|
| 1:13:54| Well, this is no longer a possibility,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4434)|
| 1:13:57| because new building codes have been adopted since that house you saw that was chopped up that will prevent this from happening.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4437)|
| 1:14:05| These codes, especially the commercial code, which is applicable to a triplex and greater,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4445)|
| 1:14:11| are so much more advanced in the realm of fire safety than how older homes and multiplexes were commonly built.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4451)|
| 1:14:20| Their implementation in a conversion would be extremely invasive and infeasible to an existing older home.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4460)|
| 1:14:28| Fire-rated walls, special doors and seals, fire-rated structural connections, special duct openings,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4468)|
| 1:14:36| sprinkler system piping, sprinkler riser rooms, fire department access points, and more| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4476)|
| 1:14:42| all make this an extremely unlikely scenario and, frankly, a poor choice for an investment on the part of a developer.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4482)|

| 1:16:22| I'm here to speak in support of this application because I believe Knoxville's zoning ordinance| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4582)|
| 1:16:27| dating back more than 50 years have imposed a nontraditional and anti-urbanist spirit on the heart of Knoxville neighborhoods,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4587)|
| 1:16:35| which historically featured housing diversity, walkability, and streetcar transit oriented toward the working class.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4595)|
| 1:16:44| Although many have expressed concerns that the character of our historic neighborhoods will be compromised by the construction of middle housing types,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4604)|
| 1:16:53| I feel exactly the opposite.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4613)|
| 1:16:56| Middle housing types are specifically characteristic of our historic neighborhoods.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4616)|
| 1:17:02| However, after reviewing the proposed amendments in conjunction with city lot data provided by Knoxville-Knox County Planning,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4622)|
| 1:17:10| I am not convinced that they would result in tremendous increase in middle housing development opportunities in our city.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4630)|
| 1:17:17| The housing type with the greatest number of development opportunities are duplexes,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4637)|
| 1:17:22| which were permitted by right in the heart of Knoxville neighborhoods prior to the adoption of recode,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4642)|
| 1:17:27| though the dimensional standards were a bit different.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4647)|
| 1:17:30| Although allowing duplexes in our neighborhoods is a huge step in the right direction,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4650)|
| 1:17:34| I don't think this proposal provides much opportunity for the other middle housing types listed.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4654)|
| 1:17:41| Triplexes, for example, are typically infeasible to build due to the added cost incurred by the switch from the residential to commercial building code.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4661)|
| 1:17:50| It is unclear from the data planning has released how many lots could support a quadplex,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4670)|
| 1:17:56| but it is a significantly smaller percentage than that for duplexes and triplexes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4676)|

| 1:18:08| You might argue that these housing types are currently permitted along the corridors, so why allow them to densify our neighborhoods?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4688)|
| 1:18:17| With a 70-foot height limit in the CG2, the highest and best use of these properties is within a completely different scale.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/planning-r-399-231005?start=4697)|
